ORIGINAL REFERENCE: 
Marchitto, T.M., R. Muscheler, J.D. Ortiz, J.D. Carriquiry, 
and A. van Geen.  2010. 
Dynamical Response of the Tropical Pacific Ocean 
to Solar Forcing During the Early Holocene. 
Science, Vol. 330, pp. 1378-1381. 
DOI: 10.1126/science.1194887 

ABSTRACT: 
We present a high-resolution magnesium/calcium proxy record 
of Holocene sea surface temperature (SST) from off the west 
coast of Baja California Sur, Mexico, a region where interannual 
SST variability is dominated today by the influence of the 
El Niño-Southern Oscillation (ENSO).  Temperatures were lowest 
during the early to middle Holocene, consistent with documented 
eastern equatorial Pacific cooling and numerical model simulations 
of orbital forcing into a La Niña-like state at that time. 
The early Holocene SSTs were also characterized by millennial-scale 
fluctuations that correlate with cosmogenic nuclide proxies of 
solar variability, with inferred solar minima corresponding to 
El Niño-like (warm) conditions, in apparent agreement with the 
theoretical "ocean dynamical thermostat" response of ENSO to 
exogenous radiative forcing. 


GEOGRAPHIC REGION: Eastern Pacific 
PERIOD OF RECORD: 13KYrBP - present 


FUNDING SOURCES: 
US National Science Foundation (NSF) grants OCE-0214221 and 
OCE-0214646.  R.M. is supported by the Royal Swedish Academy 
of Sciences through a grant financed by the Knut and Alice 
Wallenberg Foundation. 


DESCRIPTION: 
High resolution Magnesium/Calcium data and reconstructed 
sea surface temperature (SST) from an Eastern Pacific 
sediment core.  Core MV99-GC41/PC14 was drilled in the 
Soledad Basin off the west coast of Baja California Sur, 
Mexico.  Mg/Ca ratios were measured on G. bulloides, 
which reflects spring upwelling. The record spans the 
Holocene and provides an ENSO signal. 

Core MV99-GC41/PC14:  25.2°N, 112.7°W, 540 m water depth.

2. 14C & 10Be

10Be flux: combined and revised from GISP2 (Finkel & Nishiizumi, J. Geophys. Res.-Oceans 102, 26699 (1997)) 
           and GRIP (Vonmoos et al., Journal of Geophysical Research-Space Physics 111, A10105 (2006)). 
Dongge Cave d18O: smoothed and filtered after Wang et al., Science 308, 854 (2005). 
Hoti Cave d18O: smoothed and filtered after Neff et al., Nature 411, 290 (2001). 
North Atlantic IRD stack: smoothed and filtered after Bond et al., Science 294, 2130 (2001).
